beginSubroutine: s32'Create_EVT_Delilah'
  exPointFReset: (PLAYER), -32760, 0
  createExChara: s32'EVT_Delilah', s32'BED', (EX_POINT_F), 3
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'EVT_DelilahInit'
  linkObjectZ: 3
  optionVoiceLipSync: 1
  stackObjectEx: (PLAYER), (STACK5), 23, (SELF)
  runOnObject: (PLAYER)
    LinkObjectAsanoLight: 9, s32'body', s32'Bedw_matress'
  endRunOnObject: 
  upon: (PRE_DRAW)
    callSubroutine: s32'ArcadeCheck'
    ifNot: Mem(ReturnValue)
      deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'ArcadeCheck'
  returnValue: 0, 0

    returnValue: 0, 1

beginSubroutine: s32'DelilahInit'
  isObjectActive: (STACK0)
  ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
    linkPawnWithAnimation: s32'dll', s32''
    enableDarkArea: 1
    createObject: s32'Delilah_HomePosition', (PLAYER)
    stackObject: (STACK0), (PREVIOUS)
    moveToObject: (STACK0)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(1)
    ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir), Val(0)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(1380000)
        setRawPositionXInBattle: 1330000
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(-1500000)
        setRawPositionXInBattle: -1550000
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(1500000)
        setRawPositionXInBattle: 1550000
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(-1380000)
        setRawPositionXInBattle: -1330000
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  isObjectActive: (STACK1)
  ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
    createObject: s32'cmnWSBDummyEx_E', (PLAYER)
    stackObject: (STACK1), (PREVIOUS)
  endIf: 
  isObjectActive: (STACK2)
  ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
    createObject: s32'cmnWSBDummyEx_P', (PLAYER)
    stackObject: (STACK2), (PREVIOUS)
  endIf: 
  linkBone: 1
  overwriteLinkBone: s32'Head_High', s32'G_Head_def', s32'body', s32'G_Head_Attach'
  overwriteLinkBone: s32'Head_high_hair', s32'G_Head_def', s32'body', s32'G_Head_Attach'
  overwriteLinkBone: s32'Head_low', s32'G_Head_def', s32'body', s32'G_Head_Attach'
  overwriteLinkBone: s32'Head_low_hair', s32'G_Head_def', s32'body', s32'G_Head_Attach'
  landingHeight: 0
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_LH_Self'
  endIf: 
  ifTrueInObject: (ENEMY), Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmnWorldSideBreak_LH_Self'
  endIf: 
  ignoreSlowdown: 1
  ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 0
  homingClear: 
  stopLinkObject: 0
  spriteSlowParam: 1, 1, 1, 0, 150, 5
  spriteSlowParamFinishStop: 1, 1, 1, 0, 150, 5
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(AdjustmentForScript2), Val(1)
    setObjectSize: 0
  endIf: 
  upon: (PRE_DRAW)
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (PRE_DRAW)
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Ultimate1_Land'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Ultimate1_Land'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 1
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Ultimate1_Air'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Ultimate1_Air'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 1
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (WALL_BREAK)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (WALL_BREAK)
    if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
        ignoreFinishStop: 1
        ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
        if: Mem(ObjReg1)
          jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_WSB_Set_BEDandDLL'
        endIf: 
        else: 
          jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_WSB_Set_onlyDLL'
        endElse: 
        ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
          linkObjectAngle: 3
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg24)
      calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X), (SELF), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), (PLAYER)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(Tmp), Val(400000)
        ifNot: Mem(ObjReg1)
          checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActLockWait'
          ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
            ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(0)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
            endIf: 
            ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_CrouchDamage'
            endIf: 
            ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(2)
              if: Mem(IsLand)
                callSubroutine: s32'DelilahCrouchCheck'
                if: Mem(ReturnValue)
                  jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_CrouchDamage'
                endIf: 
                else: 
                  jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
                endElse: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          if: Mem(IsLand)
            checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_NmlAtk6F_TypeB'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'DelilahFinalize', Val(1), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
              moveToPosTypeToPosTypeEx: (SELF), (EX_POINT_0), (SELF), (PLAYER)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActLockWait'
              ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
                callSubroutine: s32'DelilahSyncDamageCheck'
                ifNot: Mem(ReturnValue)
                  ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(0)
                    jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
                  endIf: 
                  ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
                    jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_CrouchDamage'
                  endIf: 
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Ultimate1_Land'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Ultimate1_Air'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (PLAYER_GUARD)
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg24)
      calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X), (SELF), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), (PLAYER)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(Tmp), Val(400000)
        ifNot: Mem(ObjReg1)
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(0)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
          endIf: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_CrouchDamage'
          endIf: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(2)
            if: Mem(IsLand)
              callSubroutine: s32'DelilahCrouchCheck'
              if: Mem(ReturnValue)
                jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_CrouchDamage'
              endIf: 
              else: 
                jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
              endElse: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          if: Mem(IsLand)
            checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_NmlAtk6F_TypeB'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'DelilahFinalize', Val(1), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
              moveToPosTypeToPosTypeEx: (SELF), (EX_POINT_0), (SELF), (PLAYER)
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              callSubroutine: s32'DelilahSyncDamageCheck'
              ifNot: Mem(ReturnValue)
                ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(0)
                  jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
                endIf: 
                ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
                  jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_CrouchDamage'
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Ultimate1_Land'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
        endIf: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Ultimate1_Air'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  upon: (FRAME_STEP)
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      ifNotInObject: (ENEMY), Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
        ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
          checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'HomingJump'
          ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
            checkCurrentStateName: (ENEMY), s32'HomingJump'
            ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
              ifNot: Mem(ObjReg1)
                ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(1800000)
                  setRawPositionXInBattle: 1800000
                endIf: 
                ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(PosXRaw), Val(-1800000)
                  setRawPositionXInBattle: -1800000
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal3)
      if: Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
        ifNot: Mem(ObjReg1)
          if: Mem(IsLand)
            checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
            ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
              checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
              if: Mem(Tmp)
                sendSignalToAction: s32'Delilah_StandDamage', (SIGNAL2)
              endIf: 
              else: 
                checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_CrouchDamage'
                if: Mem(Tmp)
                  sendSignalToAction: s32'Delilah_CrouchDamage', (SIGNAL2)
                endIf: 
                else: 
                  jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
                endElse: 
              endElse: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Mem(CmnCharaReg7)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
      if: Mem(BattleDoing)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(3)
      checkScreenCollision: 0
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(4)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
      ifNot: Mem(BattleDoing)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(2)
        ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
          ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
            checkScreenCollision: 1
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(3)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    checkMoveFlag: 128
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      if: Mem(ObjReg1)
        ignoreSuperFreeze: 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    checkInput: (INPUT_ANY_DOWN)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal5), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal5), Val(0)
    endElse: 
  endUpon: 
  ifNot: Mem(FuncArg0)
    haltMomentum: 1
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(FuncArg1)
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      ifNotInObject: (ENEMY), Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
        setPositionY: 0
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
    callSubroutine: s32'DelilahFinalize'
  endUpon: 
  if: Mem(ObjReg1)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_NoBlend'
  endIf: 
  callSubroutine: s32'VoiceVolumeCheck'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'DelilahFinalize'
  debugLogForScript: s32'finalize', 0, 0
  linkObjPosition: 0
  linkObjectAngle: 0
  ignoreFinishStop: 0
  isObjectActive: (STACK1)
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      deactivateObjectById: (STACK1)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  isObjectActive: (STACK2)
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
      deactivateObjectById: (STACK2)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(FuncArg1)
    if: Mem(ObjReg1)
      exPointFResetObject: (PLAYER), (PLAYER), -32760, 0
      moveToPosType: (SELF), (EX_POINT_F)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(0)
  callSubroutine: s32'DelilahDistance'
  ifNot: Mem(FuncArg0)
    callSubroutine: s32'DelilahAction'
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(FuncArg2)
    clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'DelilahDistance'
  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ObjReg0), (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand)
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Mem(IsLand)
    calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_RAW), (SELF), (PLAYER), (STACK0), (PLAYER)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Mem(Tmp)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(100000)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X), (SELF), (PLAYER_LAND), (STACK0), (PLAYER_LAND)
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Mem(Tmp)
  calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X_FRONT), (SELF), (PLAYER_LAND), (STACK0), (PLAYER_LAND)
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Mem(Tmp)
  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ObjReg4), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg4), Mem(Dir)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(0)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyFrontDistance), Val(0)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(0)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(0)
    endElse: 
  endElse: 
  ifNot: Mem(FuncArg0)
    if: Mem(ObjReg1)
      linkObjectZ: 3
    endIf: 
    else: 
      calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_RAW), (SELF), (PLAYER_LAND), (STACK0), (PLAYER_LAND)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Mem(Tmp)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(10000)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(0)
        if: Mem(PlayerVal2)
          linkObjectZ: 0
          zLine: (NEAREST_DISTANCE), 5
        endIf: 
        else: 
          linkObjectZ: 3
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        linkObjectZ: 0
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(300000)
          zLine: (NEAREST_DISTANCE), 5
        endIf: 
        else: 
          zLine: (FAR_DISTANCE), 5
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(0)
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    linkObjectZ: 0
    zLine: (FAR_DISTANCE), 5
  endElse: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(10000)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(80000)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(0)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'BedPositionLink'
  linkObjPosition: 0
  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
  moveToObject: (PLAYER)
endSubroutine:

  endIf:

    checkLastStateName: s32'Delilah_WallHaritsukiGetUp'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf:

    if: Mem(Tmp)
      returnValue: 0, 1
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifNot: Mem(FuncArg1)
      ifNot: Mem(FuncArg0)
        checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Crouch'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          returnValue: 0, 1
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_CrouchDamage'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_CrouchTurn'
      if: Mem(Tmp)

beginSubroutine: s32'DelilahAction'
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActEntryWait'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    displayModel: 0
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(ObjReg1)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(80000)
      if: Mem(PlayerVal4)
        if: Mem(ObjReg4)
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
            callSubroutine: s32'DelilahCrouchCheck'
            if: Mem(ReturnValue)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(104)
            endIf: 
            else: 
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(3)
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(3)
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(0)
            storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
          endIf: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(1)
            checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBDown2Stand'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
            endIf: 
            checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFDown2Stand'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
            endIf: 
            checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActQuickDown2Stand'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
            endIf: 
            if: Mem(ObjReg7)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
            endIf: 
            else: 
              ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal5), Val(10)
                storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(102)
              endIf: 
              else: 
                storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
              endElse: 
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerStance), Val(2)
            storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
          endIf: 
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        if: Mem(ObjReg4)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(6)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(5)
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(80000)
      if: Mem(ObjReg4)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(6)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFDash'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(7)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(5)
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(280000)
      checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_FDash'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_FDashScared'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      if: Mem(ObjReg7)
        if: Mem(ObjReg4)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(8)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(7)
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        if: Mem(ObjReg4)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(6)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(5)
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(350000)
      if: Mem(ObjReg4)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(8)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(7)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperationInObject: (IS_GREATER), (PLAYER), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(10)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(0)
      if: Mem(ObjReg4)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(3)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(-100000)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(3)
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(3)
        callSubroutine: s32'DelilahCrouchCheck'
        if: Mem(ReturnValue)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(104)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER), (PLAYER), Mem(FrontWallDistance), Val(300000)
      if: Mem(PlayerVal4)
        ifNot: Mem(ObjReg4)
          checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFWalk'
          if: Mem(Tmp)
            storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(5)
          endIf: 
          checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFDash'
          if: Mem(Tmp)
            storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(7)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER), (PLAYER), Mem(BackWallDistance), Val(100000)
      if: Mem(PlayerVal4)
        checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActBWalk'
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          if: Mem(ObjReg4)
            storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(6)
          endIf: 
          else: 
            storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(3)
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
      checkCurrentStateName: (SELF), s32'Delilah_Hizakuzure'
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand), Val(1)
          ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(3)
            storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(11)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(100)
        callSubroutine: s32'DelilahCrouchCheck'
        if: Mem(ReturnValue)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(9)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(1)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Stand'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(102)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Crouch'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(3)
        jumpToState: s32'Delilah_StandTurn'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(104)
        jumpToState: s32'Delilah_CrouchTurn'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(5)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_FWalk'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(6)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_FWalkScared'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(7)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_FDash'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(8)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_FDashScared'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(9)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Crouch2Stand'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(10)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Scared_Land'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(11)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_KO'
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Stand'
    endElse: 
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Val(0)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'Delilah_FDash'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    debugLogForScript: s32'Delilah_FDash', 0, 0
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'DelilahInit', Val(1), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
    linkObjPosition: 0
    upon: (IDLING)
      callSubroutine: s32'DelilahDistance'
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(160000)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(100000)
          homing: (ACCELERATE_TO_SPEED), (STACK0), (PLAYER_LAND), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 10000, 0, 1000
        endIf: 
        else: 
          homing: (ACCELERATE_TO_SPEED), (STACK0), (PLAYER_LAND), 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 7000, 0, 1000
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        if: Mem(PlayerVal4)
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER), (PLAYER), Mem(FrontWallDistance), Val(300000)
            checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActFDash'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf:

          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(10000)
            homingClear: 
            haltMomentum: 1
          endIf: 
        endIf:

          ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(40)

              homingClear: 
              jumpToState: s32'Delilah_FDashStop'
            endIf: 
            else: 
              jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_FWalk'
            endElse: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_FWalk'
          endElse: 
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(SpeedX), Val(0)
        callSubroutine: s32'DelilahFinalize'
      endIf:

        if: Mem(ObjReg4)
          homingClear: 
          haltMomentum: 1
          jumpToState: s32'Delilah_StandTurn'
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(EnemyFrontDistance), Val(0)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_FDashScared'
      endElse: 
    endUpon: 
    checkLastStateName: s32'Delilah_FDashScared'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
    endIf: 
  endUpon:

  sprite: s32'dll032_01', 3

beginSubroutine: s32'DamageLoopControl'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'type1_loop2'
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'type2_loop2'
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'type3_loop2'
    endIf: 
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'type1_loop1'
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'type2_loop1'
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'type3_loop1'
    endIf: 
    haltMomentum: 1
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'VoiceVolumeCheck'
  StaticSoundVolume: 0, 100

    StaticSoundVolume: 0, 90
  endIf:

    StaticSoundVolume: 0, 80
  endIf:

  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(1100000)
    StaticSoundVolume: 0, 70
  endIf:

    StaticSoundVolume: 0, 60
  endIf: 
  calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X), (SELF), (PLAYER_LAND), (STACK0), (PLAYER_LAND)

    StaticSoundVolume: 0, 50
  endIf:

    StaticSoundVolume: 0, 40
  endIf:

  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(1500000)
    StaticSoundVolume: 0, 30
  endIf:

    StaticSoundVolume: 0, 20

endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'Delilah_StandDamage'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    debugLogForScript: s32'Delilah_StandDamage', 0, 0
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(5)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'DelilahInit', Val(0), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
    haltMomentum: 1
    homingClear: 
    linkObjPosition: 0
    ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamageOrGuard)
      ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamage)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(0)
    endElse: 
    setRandom: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1), Val(3)
    callSubroutine: s32'Delilah_StandDamage_order'
    callSubroutine: s32'DamageVoiceCheck'
    checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActWallHaritsuki'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      if: Mem(ObjReg1)
        jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_WallHaritsuki'
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(3)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(AdjustmentForScript1), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(AdjustmentForScript1), Val(2)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(AdjustmentForScript1), Val(3)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
    endIf: 
    upon: (IDLING)
      callSubroutine: s32'DelilahDistance'
      if: Mem(ActReg4)
        ifNot: Mem(CmnCharaReg24)
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg3), Val(-400000)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_StandTurn'
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
        if: Mem(ActReg3)
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_GREATER), (PLAYER), Mem(PosY), Val(0)
            storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
            storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
            storeValue: Mem(PosY), Val(0)
          endIf: 
          ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamageOrGuard)
            calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X), (SELF), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), (PLAYER)
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(Tmp), Val(400000)
              callSubroutine: s32'DamageLoopControl'
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(100000)
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(IsLand), Val(1)
            jumpToStateIfNotSame: s32'Delilah_Hizakuzure'
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (PRE_FRAME_STEP)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(13)
        callSubroutine: s32'BedPositionLink'
        storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(0)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(2)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(0)
        setAlphaColor: 255
      endIf: 
      if: Mem(CmnCharaReg24)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      if: Mem(ActReg6)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(20)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(10)
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(0)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(0)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(15)
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(4)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(0)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(11)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(PosX), (PLAYER), Mem(PosX)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(Dir), (PLAYER), Mem(Dir)
          addPositionX: 0, 600000
          faceOpponent: 
          storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg24), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(5)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (SIGNAL0)
      callSubroutine: s32'DamageLoopControl'
      callSubroutine: s32'Delilah_StandDamage_order'
    endUpon: 
    upon: (SIGNAL2)
      callSubroutine: s32'DamageLoopControl'
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(3)
    endUpon: 
    checkLastStateName: s32'Delilah_Ultimate1_Land'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(4)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      faceOpponent: 
    endElse: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
    endIf:

      displayMesh: s32'siwa_add', 1
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  gotoIfOperation: s32'type1', (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
  gotoIfOperation: s32'type2', (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
  gotoIfOperation: s32'type3', (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
  gotoIfOperation: s32'Ultimate_After', (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(4)

  setSpriteTime: 5, Mem(ActReg5)

      endElse: 
    endIf:

      setVoiceChannel: 1

  setSpriteTime: 5, Mem(ActReg5)
  sprite: s32'dll050_07', 4
  setSpriteTime: 5, Mem(ActReg5)
  sprite: s32'dll050_08', 4
  setSpriteTime: 5, Mem(ActReg5)
  sprite: s32'dll050_09', 4
  setSpriteTime: 5, Mem(ActReg5)
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'type1_loop2'
  sprite: s32'dll050_10', 20
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  endLabel: 
  if: Mem(ActReg5)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg5), Val(-1)
  endIf:

  endIf:

  addPositionX: 0, 30000
  sprite: s32'dll050_18', 4

  endLabel: 
  gotoLabelIf: s32'type1', Mem(CmnCharaReg24)
  sprite: s32'keep', 2147483647
  callSubroutine: s32'DelilahFinalize'
  endLabel: 
  exitState:

beginState: s32'Delilah_KO'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    debugLogForScript: s32'Delilah_KO', 0, 0
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(10)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'DelilahInit', Val(0), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
    haltMomentum: 1
    homingClear: 
    linkObjPosition: 0
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(100000)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    upon: (IDLING)
      calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X_FRONT), (SELF), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), (PLAYER)
      callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'DelilahDistance', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
      callSubroutine: s32'EnemyWin_PositionLink'
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  gotoLabelIf: s32'Check', Mem(ActReg0)
  sprite: s32'dll051_00', 3
  sprite: s32'dll051_01', 4
  sprite: s32'dll051_02', 4
  sprite: s32'dll051_03', 4
  sprite: s32'dll051_04', 4
  sprite: s32'dll051_05', 4
  sprite: s32'dll051_06', 4
  sprite: s32'dll051_07', 4
  sprite: s32'dll051_08', 4
  sprite: s32'dll051_09', 4
  sprite: s32'dll051_10', 4
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'distCheck'
  sprite: s32'dll051_11', 30
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(300000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabelIf: s32'Check', Mem(ActReg0)

        boneRotation: s32'Head_Attach', 33333, 0, 50000, 1, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0

        boneRotation: s32'Head_Attach', 57111, 3000, 30000, 3, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0
        boneRotation: s32'chest', 2000, 0, 5000, 3, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0
      endIf:

        faceEye: 2, 3, 1, 1
        faceBrow: 2, 3, 1, 1
        faceMouth: 2, 3, 1, 1

        faceEye: 3, 9, 1, 1
        faceBrow: 3, 9, 1, 1
        faceMouth: 3, 9, 1, 1
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(42)
        boneRotation: s32'chest', 0, 0, 0, 12, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0
        boneRotation: s32'Head_Attach', 0, 0, 0, 9, (ACTV_ACTIVE), 0, 0

          onSpriteChange: s32'dll401_00'
        endIf:

          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
          jumpToState: s32'Delilah_AirEscape_After'
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Special1_Air'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Special2_Air'
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)

      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon:

beginState: s32'Delilah_AirEscape_After'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)

    if: Mem(Tmp)
      ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 1
      addPositionX: 0, -70000

        clearRegisteredUponCode: (AFTER_EXIT)
        ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 0
      endUpon:

    upon: (IDLING)
      callSubroutine: s32'DelilahDistance'

    upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      haltMomentum: 1
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'land'
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'dll424_00', 3
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg24)
    addPositionX: 0, -100000
    addPositionY: 0, -20000

    addPositionY: 0, -50000

  endLabel:

  sprite: s32'dll424_01', 3
  sprite: s32'dll424_02', 3
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabel: s32'loop'

  sprite: s32'dll424_04', 3
  sprite: s32'dll424_05', 3
  sprite: s32'dll424_06', 3

    ifNot: Mem(SentToObject0)
      upon: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
        deactivateObjectByName: s32'AddObj_MarkingObj'
        gotoLabelRequests: s32'damage'
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 600
  stackObjectEx: (SELF), (STACK0), 3, (STACK2)
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
      moveObjectToCollisionPoint: (PLAYER), 13, 1
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
      warp: (STACK0), (PLAYER), Val(0), Val(0), Val(8)
      upon: (IDLING)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(5)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          haltMomentum: 1
          moveToPosType: (STACK0), (PLAYER)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'burst'
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'burst'
  sprite: s32'null', 40
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
  callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmnWSB_Effect_NoStop_or_Delete', Val(0), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
  ifNot: Mem(SentToObject0)
    createObject: s32'Special1_AddObj', (PLAYER)
    createObject: s32'BED_400_firing', (PLAYER)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    createObject: s32'Special1_AddObjULT', (PLAYER)
    createObject: s32'BED_400_Exfiring', (PLAYER)
  endElse: 
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
  deactivateObjectByName: s32'AddObj_MarkingObj'
  endLabel:

    endIf: 
    else:

      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(600000)
        stackObjectEx: (SELF), (STACK0), 14, (ATTACKER)
        isObjectActive: (STACK0)
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          ifTrueInObject: (STACK0), Mem(IsPlayer)
            ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (STACK1), Mem(ObjReg2), Val(100000)

              endIf:

          endIf:
